This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
SRI  LANKA  INSTITUTE  OF  ARCHITECTS
New Registration and Renewal of Registration of “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural Licentiates”
for the Year 2015/2016 under the Architects  Registration Board, established as per the Sri Lanka Institute of
Architects (Amendment) Act, No 14 of 1996
REFERENCE is made to the notes appearing on pages 1A, 2A, 3A, 4A  and 5A of the Gazette of the Democratic Socialist
Republic of Sri Lanka (Extraordinary)  No. 1015 / 19 of Friday, the 20 th February, 1998 with regard to the Registration of
persons who are eligible to practice Architecture in Sri Lanka under the Categories “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and
Architectural “Licentiates”. The interpretations of the Sri Lanka Institute of Architects (Amendment) Act, No. 14 of 1996 in the
above Gazette Notification will apply in all respects to the list published below.
The Architects Registration Board of the Sri Lanka Institute of Architects as per  the functions and  powers vested
upon it by the said Act, of Parliament has now prepared the list of the “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural
Licentiates” who are eligible to be Gazetted for the Year 2015/2016 (01st February 2015 to 31st January 2016).
The Architects Registration Board directed me to publish the Names,  Addresses  and Registration Numbers of the
“Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural Licentiates”  who have been registered as given below.
This registration expires on 31st January, 2016.
E. G. G. M. E
LLEPOLAGEDARA,
Registrar,
Architects Registration Board.
Sri Lanka Institute of Architects,
No. 120/7, Vidya Mawatha, Colombo 07,
26th January 2015.
